#President Xi Visits Myanmar
country_event = {
	id = china.3
	title = china.3.t
	desc = china.3.d
	picture = GFX_PRC_Myanmar
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
	}
	option = {
		name = china.3.a
		add_political_power = 10
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = BRM
			modifier = state_visit
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = global.PRC_influence_BRM_var_temp
			value = 0.05
		}
		PRC_add_BRM_influence = yes
	}
}

#Oil Crash Hits China
country_event = {
	id = china.4
	title = china.4.t
	desc = china.4.d
	picture = GFX_red_line_go_down
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PRC_oil_crisis_ongoing
			country_event = {
				id = china.11
				days = 5
			}
			add_ideas = PRC_oil_crash1
			add_political_power = -30
			country_event = {
				id = china.288
				days = 3
			}
			country_event = {
				id = china.289
				days = 30
			}
			country_event = {
				id = china.290
				days = 40
			}
			country_event = {
				id = china.324
				days = 110
			}
			add_stability = -0.25
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist
				popularity = -0.175
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = china.4.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = PRC_oil_crash1
			add_political_power = -30
		}
		focus_unlock = yes
	}
}

#Taiwan war victory
country_event = {
	id = china.23
	title = china.23.t
	desc = {
		text = china.23.d.1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = PRC_taiwanese_government_captured
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = china.23.d.2
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PRC_taiwanese_government_captured
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_event_taiwanwarwin
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = PRC
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {

			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_1	
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_2
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_3
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_4
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_5
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_6
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_7
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_8
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_9
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_10
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_11
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_12
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_13
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_14
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_15
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_16
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_17
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_18
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_19
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_20	
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_21	
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_22	
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_23	
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_24	
			remove_ideas = taihaijingji_idea_25
			transfer_state = 524
			transfer_state = 1150
			transfer_state = 1149
			transfer_state = 1148
			if = {
				limit = {
					controls_state = 876
				}
				transfer_state = 876
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
			set_global_flag = PRC_taiwan_war_won
			set_country_flag = PRC_centrist_win
			PRC_end_taiwan_war = yes
			annex_country = {
				target = CHI
				transfer_troops = no
			}
			set_country_leader_portrait = {
				ideology = nationalist
				portrait = GFX_portrait_PRC_xi_jinping_taiwan_win
			}
			news_event = {
				id = news.356
				hours = 12
			}
			news_event = {
				id = china.80
				days = 70
			}
			load_focus_tree = china_centrist_focus
			AST = {
				country_event = {
					id = Australia.1
					days = 15
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = CHI
					NOT = {
						state = 524
						state = 1150
						state = 1149
						state = 1148
					}
				}
				remove_claim_by = CHI
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = china.23.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			focus_unlock = yes
			transfer_state = 524
			transfer_state = 1150
			transfer_state = 1149
			transfer_state = 1148
			if = {
				limit = {
					controls_state = 876
				}
				transfer_state = 876
			}
			add_war_support = 0.05
		}
	}
}

				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = PRC_special_political_zones

					days = 14

		}
	}

	id = china.187
	title = china.187.t
	desc = china.187.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	option = { #Hardliners Take Over
		name = china.187.a
		trigger = {
			is_power_balance_in_range = {
				id = PRC_Liberal_Conservative_power_balance
				range < PRC_balance_range
			}
		}
		retire_character = PRC_wang_yang
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = communist
			long_name = PRC_communist_party_liberals_na_long
			name = PRC_communist_party_liberals_na
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = PRC_Xie_Fuzhan
			ideology = left_nationalism
		}
	}
	option = { #Reformists Take Over
		name = china.187.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_power_balance_in_range = {
					id = PRC_Liberal_Conservative_power_balance
					range > PRC_balance_range
				}
				is_power_balance_in_range = {
					id = PRC_Liberal_Conservative_power_balance
					range = PRC_balance_range
				}
			}
		}
		retire_character = PRC_wang_yang
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = communist
			long_name = PRC_communist_party_liberals_nd_long
			name = PRC_communist_party_liberals_nd
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = PRC_Liu_Qibao
			ideology = neo_socialism
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

				add_idea = PRC_plan_dummy
				remove_idea = PRC_plan_dummy_7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = PRC_taiwan_war_countdown
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
	 			mission = PRC_taiwan_war_countdown
 				days = 15
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {
						has_active_mission = JAP_taiwan_war_mission
					}
				}
				JAP = {
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
						mission = JAP_taiwan_war_mission
						days = 15
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = PRC_positioning_dynamic_var
				value = 0.05
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = PRC_screening_efficiency_dynamic_var
				value = 0.1
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = PRC_spotting_chance_dynamic_var
				value = 0.1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = china.268
	title = china.268.t
	desc = {
		text = china.268.d.1
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = PRC_project_swimmer_succeeded
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = china.268.d.2
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = PRC_project_swimmer_failed
		}
	}
	desc = china.268.d
	picture = GFX_PRC_swimmer
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = PRC_military_project_researching
	}
	option = {
		name = china.268.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = PRC_project_swimmer_succeeded
		}
		set_country_flag = PRC_project_swimmer_succeeded1
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = advanced_medium_tank_chassis
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
			    advanced_medium_tank_chassis = 1
			}
		}
		set_technology = {
		    amphibious_drive = 1
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			name = "ZTZ-105 ''Swimmer''"
			type = modern_tank_chassis_3
			parent_version = 0
			modules = {
				main_armament_slot = tank_high_velocity_cannon_3
				turret_type_slot = tank_modern_tank_turret
				suspension_type_slot = tank_torsion_bar_suspension
				armor_type_slot = tank_riveted_armor
				engine_type_slot = tank_gasoline_engine
				special_type_slot_1 = tank_radio_1
				special_type_slot_2 = amphibious_drive
				special_type_slot_3 = auto_loader
				special_type_slot_4 = smoke_launchers
				special_type_slot_5 = gunner_thermal_1
				special_type_slot_6 = extra_ammo_storage
			}
			upgrades = {
				tank_nsb_engine_upgrade = 9
				tank_nsb_armor_upgrade = 3
			}
			icon = "GFX_PRC_ztz_105"
		}
		add_equipment_production = {
			equipment = {
				type = modern_tank_chassis_3
				creator = "PRC" 
				version_name = "ZTZ-105 "Swimmer""
			}
			requested_factories = 10
			efficiency = 100
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = PRC_swimmer
			bonus = 0.35
			uses = 1
			category = armor
		}
		army_experience = 25
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = PRC_army_reform_progress_temp
			value = 0.02
		}
		PRC_add_army_reform_progress = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = china.268.b
		add_political_power = 25
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = PRC_project_nib_failed
		}
		set_country_flag = PRC_project_nib_failed1
		set_technology = {
		    amphibious_drive = 1
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = PRC_swimmer
			bonus = 0.15
			uses = 1
			category = armor
		}
	}

			}
		}

			allow_without_tech = yes

				fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_1 = recon_camera

				special_type_slot_1 = hmg_defense_turret
				special_type_slot_2 = ai_targeting_computer_small
				special_type_slot_3 = radio_navigation_1

			target = BAN
			type = annex_everything
		}

			limit = {
				JAP = {
					has_war_with = PRC
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				add_to_faction = BAN
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					JAP = {
						has_war_with = PRC
					}
				}
			}
			RAJ = {
				add_to_faction = BAN
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					RAJ = {
						has_war_with = PRC
					}
					JAP = {
						has_war_with = PRC
					}
				}
			}
			AST = {
				add_to_faction = BAN
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = china.285.b
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

#Dragon in the Sky
country_event = {
	id = china.500
	title = china.500.t
	desc = china.500.d
	picture = GFX_PRC_chengdu_j_36
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = PRC_military_project_researching
	}
	option = {
		name = china.500.a
		air_experience = 25
		set_country_flag = PRC_project_song_wencong_succeeded1
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_tech = modern_small_airframe
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
			    modern_small_airframe = 1
			}
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			name = "Chengdu J-36"
			type = small_plane_airframe_4
			modules = {
				fixed_main_weapon_slot = aircraft_cannon_1_1x
				fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_1 = aircraft_cannon_1_1x
				fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_2 = aircraft_cannon_1_1x
				fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_3 = aircraft_cannon_1_1x
				fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_4 = aircraft_cannon_1_1x
				engine_type_slot = engine_4_2x
				special_type_slot_1 = hmg_defense_turret
				special_type_slot_2 = ai_targeting_computer_small
				special_type_slot_3 = radio_navigation_2
				special_type_slot_4 = fuel_tanks_small
				special_type_slot_5 = lmg_defense_turret_2x
			}
			icon = "GFX_PRC_j_36_eq2"
		}
		add_equipment_production = {
			equipment = {
				type = small_plane_airframe_4
				creator = "PRC" 
				version_name = "Chengdu J-36"
			}
			requested_factories = 10
			efficiency = 100
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = small_plane_airframe_4
			variant_name = "Chengdu J-36"
			amount = 50
			producer = PRC
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PRC_project_song_wencong_succeeded_tt
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = PRC_song_wencong
			bonus = 1
			uses = 1
			category = light_air
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = PRC_army_reform_progress_temp
			value = 0.035
		}
		PRC_add_army_reform_progress = yes
	}
}

				}

					add_days_mission_timeout = {
		 				mission = JAP_taiwan_war_mission
						days = -250
					}
				}
				CHI = {
					add_days_mission_timeout = {
		 				mission = CHI_taiwan_war_mission
						days = -250
					}
				}
			}

				add_ideas = PRC_fatal_mistake_idea
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = china.666.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = CHI
				}
				add_ideas = PRC_fatal_mistake_idea

	 				mission = PRC_taiwan_war_countdown
 					days = -250
				}
			}

		}
	}
